< Review>
Good food at a reasonable price. This place is near my work, so I've eaten here many times. They have all the popular Thai dishes in lunch or dinner portions. They have an $8 lunch special with chicken, seafood, beef, pork or vegetarian options, so there's something for everyone. They serve soups, noodles, rice or curries. Their appetizers are also very good. They accommodate small or large parties easily, and orders come out very quickly. If you're in the area looking for a Thai fix, give Exotic Thai a try (no pun intended).< /Review>

I stopped in here to see what it was all about. I am a big fan of Bronx pizza and I want to see how this would compare. I must say I am a fan of this restaurant. I will not go as far as to say it is the same as Bronx pizza because this is more of a Long Island style. The sauce is great the crust is great and the toppings are of a high quality. I like the fact that they have regular Italian style thin crust pizza as well as Sicilian pizza. The white stone is good the pepperoni mushroom was excellent and I also like the fact that they have garlic powder, parmesan as well and red chili flakes for you to put on your pizza. When I ordered my slice the employees here notice that the pizza was already  a little old so they made me fresh slices. This really shows the type of customer service that is needed in any service industry. I would recommend this pizza place and I will be back. The lady that was working at the front Ashley was very nice and very helpful. The gentleman that was cooking the pizzas name was Adrian he was the one that noticed that the pizza that they were going to serve me was a bit old so they made fresh ones. That to me shows the attention to detail that is needed. I am very happy with the service.<//review>
